name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Double Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted December 22, 2023
msg:We liked the hotel location and amenities, especially the self-service laundry room and the late night noodles in the dining room. The hotel is conveniently located next to a big shopping mall (KK One) and has a subway station right in front. Many food options and coffee shops nearby. 

The only caveat is the check-in experience. When we arrived at the check in time, the hotel receptionist said we couldn't check in because the previous guest hadn't checked out. And they recommend we purchase the Atour membership for ~280 RMB to get an upgraded room so that we can check in now, otherwise we'd have to wait indefinitely for the previous guest to check out. This seems scammy. We complained to Trip.com and they helped us resolve it with the hotel who then gave us the upgrade for free.

Fortunately, the hotel is conveniently located and can be reached by foot from Line 9 Xiasha Station. When I got out of the subway, I forgot which exit the front desk guy told me to take. I followed the flow of people and walked to Exit A by feeling, only to see that the hotel sign was actually opposite! ! ! I tried to call the front desk to ask if they could come pick me up. Unexpectedly, the little brother didn't hesitate and agreed immediately. It took me a few minutes to find me, and took the initiative to help me pull the suitcase. name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Executive Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted April 1, 2024
msg:I was so impressed by the hotel's first-class service that I had to write my first comment.
In terms of geography: As soon as I got off the subway, I saw that the hotel entrance is very convenient. It is isolated and there are many places to eat, drink and have fun. It feels super right.
Room: The hygiene is very good, and the drinks and biscuits provided in the refrigerator are thoughtful and not fussy (I personally find it annoying for hotels to provide paid drinks, and they often end up being charged for the wrong drinks afterwards...). The room is so big, the view is open and the space feels great! The only thing is that the semi-scrubbed bathroom is a bit embarrassing for children😅
In terms of service: Upon checkin, a cup of hot tea is the first thing to relax and soothe after a long journey. Checkout also comes with two bottles of water, which is very heartwarming!
It's super convenient to add WeChat at the front desk for direct inquiries. Fuyu's answers are quick and detailed.
I thought the free late-night snack was just because the porridge contained a lot of food, and when I was full, I couldn't help but eat again.
There was a member at the front desk who told me that I could delay check-out to 6pm and get breakfast. 200 yuan is actually OK, and discounts are available for several stays, but I don’t know when I will be back in Li, so I don’t want to join. In the end, they all got breakfast for 2 adults and 2 children! It turns out that the breakfast room was so full at 9 o'clock, with 4 people waiting in line for the first table.
The guy at the door was dressed as a chef, and his mobility was amazing! First of all, because there were so many people, he kept saying that he was sorry to have to wait. He was so sincere and made people think that if he had to wait, he would just wait. In addition, he really wanted to solve the problem and asked me if I would mind if he moved my little girl to Taiwan. I was fine with adding tables and space, but he personally went to the isolation meeting room and moved 4 small tables and added chairs in one go. Suddenly, the queue of people had to sit down and eat. I really have to praise him. services. In addition to taking a seat and seeing him busy, he also carried juice to refill, etc. It was a versatile place to watch!
All in all, the service is very impressive. A cup of tea and a bottle of water are not worth much. It is often remembered by guests because of their small considerate service. I am willing to help promote it. I hope it will continue to be the same and I will have the opportunity to come back in the future!

在全國各地出差旅行時，都會首選亞朵。在此期間我也感受過很多酒店和業主方帶來的優秀服務體驗。但是深圳濱河亞朵這兩天帶來的快速響應、用心接待，超預期善良暖心舉動讓我驚喜又感動！
因為我帶着年邁的母親和我的小兒子來到深圳玩，在辦理入住後我便帶着母親和兒子上樓存放行李，我便下樓匆匆去買水果給母親。當我買完水果之後發現母親和前台的章陽在酒店門口等我。還沒等我開口，章陽主動告知我，母親見我下樓便跟隨我一起下來尋找我（母親有些許的老年痴呆），回來的時候外面下着雨，章陽夥伴在外打着傘並安慰長者家就在門口等我。當我得知這個消息時，我非常感激與感謝！善意的一舉幫我解決了不少沒必要的麻煩和問題！
我深刻的感受到亞朵的善良與忠心的服務，很高興酒店能珍視培養出這一羣年輕又活力善良的小可愛們，讓我更堅定、執着的選擇亞朵！成為亞朵的一枚鐵粉。
再次感謝深圳濱河時代亞朵酒店，我會持續入住並保持良好的心情去體驗更多亞朵的熱情服務與善良！！

酒店表示有其他客人反應中央冷氣太冷

早餐據説是38還是28元一位，在攜程買含早餐的房似乎更貴。
圖為酒店入口。

總之如果你不知道深圳訂什麼酒店 不想踩雷 這家雖然沒有到盡善盡美 但起碼不會出錯 沒有什麼大的問題。

msg:職員十分友善，房間check in非常快速，但問題是我與太太二人居住，但竟然編配了一個衹有一張椅嘅房間，以致我太太沒有地方坐，要坐在床上或距離遠的書枱那邊。

在我吃完午飯回來後便要求調房，職員最初説沒有，但擾攘一番後又找到了一間，可惜是有煙味的房間，但亦沒有辦法。

另外稱心的就是免費洗衣哪個部分， 酒店所提供的洗衣機與乾衣機型號很細小，與V-Park 阿朵所提供的大機完全不可比較， 由於洗衣機及乾衣機均很細，可洗嘅衫量及乾衫量相對便很少， 觀乎V-Park阿朵提供的則很大，洗衣乾衣都很有效率，通常少於一小時內便可洗完衣服，再放進乾衣機一小時便完全乾透。但這間阿朵乾衣機操作實在太多選擇，我選擇「乾透」模式操作了兩小時半後取出發覺衹是乾了六七成，但由於巳是凌晨一小時，唯有帶回房用衣架掛在房間或鋪在枱椅上晾乾， 整體感覺很沮喪，對阿朵印像變差了，下次不會再到深圳亞朵，衹會去中山。
